     1 import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
     2 
     3 interface CacheOptions {
     4   ttl?: number; // Time to live in milliseconds
     5   key: string;
     6 }
     7 
     8 interface CacheEntry<T> {
     9   data: T;
    10   timestamp: number;
    11 }
    12 
    13 const cache = new Map<string, CacheEntry<any>>();
    14 
    15 export function useCache<T>(
    16   fetchFn: () => Promise<T>,
    17   options: CacheOptions
    18 ) {
    19   const { ttl = 60000, key } = options; // Default 1 minute
    20   const [data, setData] = useState<T | null>(null);
    21   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    22   const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null);
    23 
    24   const fetchData = useCallback(async (forceRefresh = false) => {
    25     // 检查缓存
    26     if (!forceRefresh) {
    27       const cached = cache.get(key);
    28       if (cached && Date.now() - cached.timestamp < ttl) {
    29         setData(cached.data);
    30         return cached.data;
    31       }
    32     }
    33 
    34     setLoading(true);
    35     setError(null);
    36 
    37     try {
    38       const result = await fetchFn();
    39       cache.set(key, { data: result, timestamp: Date.now() });
    40       setData(result);
    41       return result;
    42     } catch (err) {
    43       setError(err as Error);
    44       throw err;
    45     } finally {
    46       setLoading(false);
    47     }
    48   }, [fetchFn, key, ttl]);
    49 
    50   const invalidate = useCallback(() => {
    51     cache.delete(key);
    52   }, [key]);
    53 
    54   useEffect(() => {
    55     fetchData();
    56   }, [fetchData]);
    57 
    58   return {
    59     data,
    60     loading,
    61     error,
    62     refetch: fetchData,
    63     invalidate,
    64   };
    65 }
    66 
    67 // 清除所有缓存
    68 export function clearAllCache() {
    69   cache.clear();
    70 }
    71 
    72 // 清除特定前缀的缓存
    73 export function clearCacheByPrefix(prefix: string) {
    74   for (const key of cache.keys()) {
    75     if (key.startsWith(prefix)) {
    76       cache.delete(key);
    77     }
    78   }
    79 }
    80

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-b5vwlh6eky69/src/lib/cache.ts:
     1 /**
     2  * 极简 API 缓存层
     3  */
     4 
     5 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     6 import { storage } from './storage';
     7 
     8 const memoryCache = new Map<string, { data: any, timestamp: number }>();
     9 const ongoingRequests = new Map<string, Promise<any>>();
    10 
    11 let hitQueue: { recordKey: string, isHit: boolean }[] = [];
    12 let hitTimeout: any = null;
    13 const recentlyRecorded = new Set<string>();
    14 
    15 const flushHits = async () => {
    16   if (hitQueue.length === 0) return;
    17   const batch = [...hitQueue];
    18   hitQueue = [];
    19   hitTimeout = null;
    20   
    21   try {
    22     // 按照 recordKey 进行去重，同一个批次内同一个 key 只记一次
    23     const uniqueBatch = batch.filter((item, index, self) => 
    24       index === self.findIndex((t) => t.recordKey === item.recordKey)
    25     );
    26 
    27     await Promise.all(uniqueBatch.map(item => 
    28       (supabase.rpc as any)('record_cache_hit', { p_cache_key: item.recordKey, p_is_hit: item.isHit })
    29     ));
    30   } catch (e: any) {
    31     console.warn('[Cache Stats Error]', e.message);
    32   }
    33 };
    34 
    35 export const cache = {
    36   get<T>(key: string, ttl: number = 60000, recordKey?: string): T | null {
    37     const now = Date.now();
    38     
    39     // 1. 优先尝试内存缓存
    40     const cached = memoryCache.get(key);
    41     if (cached && (now - cached.timestamp <= ttl)) {
    42       this._recordStats(recordKey, true);
    43       return cached.data as T;
    44     }
    45 
    46     // 2. 尝试持久化缓存 (模拟 SDK 行为)
    47     const persisted = storage.get<{data: T, timestamp: number} | null>(`api_cache_${key}`, null);
    48     if (persisted && (now - persisted.timestamp <= ttl)) {
    49       // 填补内存缓存
    50       memoryCache.set(key, persisted);
    51       this._recordStats(recordKey, true);
    52       return persisted.data as T;
    53     }
    54 
    55     this._recordStats(recordKey, false);
    56 
    57     // 后台管理页面禁用缓存，确保 CRUD 实时生效
    58     if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.location.pathname.startsWith('/admin')) {
    59       return null;
    60     }
    61     
    62     return null;
    63   },
    64 
    65   set<T>(key: string, data: T, persist: boolean = false): void {
    66     const entry = { data, timestamp: Date.now() };
    67     memoryCache.set(key, entry);
    68     ongoingRequests.delete(key);
    69 
    70     if (persist) {
    71       storage.set(`api_cache_${key}`, entry);
    72     }
    73   },
    74 
    75   async getOrFetch<T>(key: string, fetchFn: () => Promise<T>, ttl: number = 60000, recordKey?: string, persist: boolean = false): Promise<T> {
    76     const cached = this.get<T>(key, ttl, recordKey);
    77     if (cached !== null) return cached;
    78 
    79     const ongoing = ongoingRequests.get(key);
    80     if (ongoing) return ongoing;
    81 
    82     const request = fetchFn().then(data => {
    83       this.set(key, data, persist);
    84       return data;
    85     }).catch(err => {
    86       ongoingRequests.delete(key);
    87       throw err;
    88     });
    89 
    90     ongoingRequests.set(key, request);
    91     return request;
    92   },
    93 
    94   _recordStats(recordKey?: string, isHit: boolean = false): void {
    95     if (recordKey && !recentlyRecorded.has(recordKey)) {
    96       recentlyRecorded.add(recordKey);
    97       // 5分钟后允许再次记录该 key
    98       setTimeout(() => recentlyRecorded.delete(recordKey), 300000);
    99 
   100       hitQueue.push({ recordKey, isHit });
   101       if (hitQueue.length >= 10) {
   102         flushHits();
   103       } else if (!hitTimeout) {
   104         hitTimeout = setTimeout(flushHits, 2000);
   105       }
   106     }
   107   },
   108 
   109   invalidate(key: string): void {
   110     memoryCache.delete(key);
   111     storage.remove(`api_cache_${key}`);
   112     ongoingRequests.delete(key);
   113   },
   114 
   115   clear(): void {
   116     memoryCache.clear();
   117   }
   118 };
   119

     1 import React, { Component, ErrorInfo, ReactNode } from 'react';
     2 import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
     3 import { AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react';
     4 
     5 interface Props {
     6   children: ReactNode;
     7 }
     8 
     9 interface State {
    10   hasError: boolean;
    11   error: Error | null;
    12 }
    13 
    14 export class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
    15   public state: State = {
    16     hasError: false,
    17     error: null
    18   };
    19 
    20   public static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
    21     return { hasError: true, error };
    22   }
    23 
    24   public componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: ErrorInfo) {
    25     console.error('[ErrorBoundary] 捕获到错误:', error, errorInfo);
    26     
    27     // 如果是动态导入模块失败，可能是因为应用版本更新导致静态资源路径失效
    28     // 这种情况下，自动刷新页面通常可以解决问题
    29     const isChunkLoadError = error.name === 'ChunkLoadError' || 
    30                            /Failed to fetch dynamically imported module/i.test(error.message) ||
    31                            /loading chunk/i.test(error.message);
    32                            
    33     if (isChunkLoadError) {
    34       const lastReloaded = sessionStorage.getItem('last_chunk_error_reload');
    35       const now = Date.now();
    36       
    37       // 避免无限循环刷新：如果 10 秒内已经刷新过，就不要再刷了
    38       if (!lastReloaded || now - parseInt(lastReloaded) > 10000) {
    39         sessionStorage.setItem('last_chunk_error_reload', now.toString());
    40         console.warn('检测到资源加载错误，正在尝试自动刷新页面...');
    41         window.location.reload();
    42       }
    43     }
    44   }
    45 
    46   public render() {
    47     if (this.state.hasError) {
    48       return (
    49         <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background p-8">
    50           <div className="max-w-md w-full bg-card rounded-2xl shadow-lg p-8 text-center">
    51             <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-destructive/10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
    52               <AlertCircle className="w-8 h-8 text-destructive" />
    53             </div>
    54             <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">应用出错了</h1>
    55             <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-6">
    56               {this.state.error?.message || '发生了未知错误'}
    57             </p>
    58             <div className="space-y-3">
    59               <Button 
    60                 onClick={() => window.location.reload()} 
    61                 className="w-full"
    62               >
    63                 刷新页面
    64               </Button>
    65               <Button 
    66                 variant="outline"
    67                 onClick={() => {
    68                   this.setState({ hasError: false, error: null });
    69                 }}
    70                 className="w-full"
    71               >
    72                 重试
    73               </Button>
    74             </div>
    75             {process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' && (
    76               <details className="mt-6 text-left">
    77                 <summary className="text-xs text-muted-foreground cursor-pointer">
    78                   查看详细错误信息
    79                 </summary>
    80                 <pre className="mt-2 text-xs bg-muted p-3 rounded overflow-auto max-h-40">
    81                   {this.state.error?.stack}
    82                 </pre>
    83               </details>
    84             )}
    85           </div>
    86         </div>
    87       );
    88     }
    89 
    90     return this.props.children;
    91   }
    92 }

AgentThinkAction(thought='我高度怀疑根本问题是 `vite.config.ts` 中 `base: \'./\'` 导致 SPA 在非根路径下懒加载 chunk 路径解析错误。\n\nVite `base: \'./\'` 会让动态导入的 chunk 使用相对路径。当浏览器在 `/admin/pc` 路径时，`./assets/xxx.js` 会被解析为 `/admin/assets/xxx.js`，而不是 `/assets/xxx.js`。如果服务器没有特别配置 `/admin/assets/*` 也指向静态资源目录，就会 fallback 到 index.html，浏览器收到 HTML 而不是 JS，解析失败导致 ChunkLoadError。\n\n从首页跳转时浏览器在 `/` 路径，相对路径 `./assets/xxx.js` → `/assets/xxx.js`，正确加载。\n\n这完美解释了为什么"只能通过首页跳转"。\n\n修复：将默认 base 从 `\'./\'` 改为 `\'/\'`。', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

CONTENT: 根据app端的app-sdk：import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { fetch } from 'expo/fetch';

/**
 * App Management SDK
 * 用于前端App对接后端配置的完整SDK
 *
 * 使用方式:
 * 1. 在后台管理 -> App管理 -> 创建App配置

/**
 * 混淆解密函数（增强版）
 * 支持两种加密格式：
 * 1. __ENC__ (旧版，简单 Base64)
 * 2. __ENC_Z__ (新版，盐值 + 反转 + Base64)
 */
const decryptStr = (str: string) => {
  if (typeof str === 'string') {
    try {
      const b64Decode = (s: string) => {
        if (typeof atob === 'function') return atob(s);
        // @ts-ignore
        const buf = typeof global !== 'undefined' ? global['Buffer'] : undefined;
        if (buf) return buf.from(s, 'base64').toString('binary');
        return s; // Fallback
      };

      // 新版混淆加密（盐值 + 反转）
      if (str.startsWith('__ENC_Z__')) {
        const reversed = str.replace('__ENC_Z__', '').split('').reverse().join('');
        const decoded = b64Decode(reversed);
        const salted = decodeURIComponent(decoded);
        // 移除盐值前缀
        const salt = 'Zingle_';
        return salted.startsWith(salt) ? salted.slice(salt.length) : salted;
      }
      
      // 旧版简单加密（向后兼容）
      if (str.startsWith('__ENC__')) {
        const decoded = b64Decode(str.replace('__ENC__', ''));
        return decodeURIComponent(decoded);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('Decryption failed:', e);
      return str;
    }
  }
  return str;
};

const BASE_URL = decryptStr('__ENC_Z__=Qnbl1WZnFmbh1WLwBXYGJTJxYnRyUycu9Wa0Nmb1ZmRyUibj5CO182duU2chJWYwV3cGJTJGJTJBNTJzBHd0h2Xlx2ZulmW');
const DEFAULT_SUPABASE_URL = decryptStr('__ENC_Z__=gGd1FWLwBXYGJTJxYnRyUycu9Wa0Nmb1ZmRyUibj5CO182duU2chJWYwV3cGJTJGJTJBNTJzBHd0h2Xlx2ZulmW');
const DEFAULT_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = decryptStr('__ENC_Z__=ElY5d2NtdDZM1UQytmbGVXRohHazs0VqN3Vh5UQjdDUPF1QPdHaq5Ub4FnL5IERNdXQE9EMJpXT1UkaPlWQIVGbKNET3FkaOpXR65EMjpnT49maJBjRXFWa3lWSs5EWZlmRHNWMO5WS2kUejpHbtl0cJlmY2VzVZl2bqlEb4JjY5pUel5SOKNkVYB3aJZTSDNWNS5WSzlUaOFTS6VVSKl2TpN2RihmS5V2Xlx2ZulmW');

// 大数据缓存存储封装 (React Native 版本)
import AsyncStorage from '@react-native-async-storage/async-storage';
import * as SecureStore from 'expo-secure-store';

const storage = {
  async setItem(key: string, value: string) {
    try {
      await AsyncStorage.setItem(key, value);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('Storage error', e);
    }
  },
  async getItem(key: string): Promise {
    try {
      return await AsyncStorage.getItem(key);
    } catch (e) {
      return null;
    }
  },
  async deleteItem(key: string) {
    try {
      await AsyncStorage.removeItem(key);
    } catch (e) {
      // ignore
    }
  }
};

// 专门用于配置的 SecureStorage
const secureStorage = {
  async setItem(key: string, value: string) {
    try {
      await SecureStore.setItemAsync(key, value);
    } catch (e) {
      // fallback
      await storage.setItem(key, value);
    }
  },
  async getItem(key: string): Promise {
    try {
      return await SecureStore.getItemAsync(key);
    } catch (e) {
      return await storage.getItem(key);
    }
  },
  async deleteItem(key: string) {
    try {
      await SecureStore.deleteItemAsync(key);
    } catch (e) {
      await storage.deleteItem(key);
    }
  }
};

  features: Record;
  api: Record;
  storage: Record;
  ui: Record;
  cfr2: Record;
  custom: Record;
  isActive: boolean;

}

  version: string;

  downloadUrl: string | null;
  installUrl: string | null;

}

export interface FeatureFlags {
  enableUpload: boolean;
  enableDiscovery: boolean;
  enableAlbum: boolean;
  enableDailyGallery: boolean;
  enablePersonalCenter: boolean;
  enableComment: boolean;
  enableShare: boolean;
  enableDownload: boolean;
  enableWatermark: boolean;
  enableAds: boolean;

  requireAuditForDiscovery: boolean;
  [key: string]: boolean;
}

export interface SdkConfig {
  appId: string;
  apiKey: string;
  baseUrl?: string;
  timeout?: number;
}

export class AppManager {
  private config: SdkConfig;
  private baseUrl: string;
  // 请求去重：同一时刻重复的请求共享同一个 Promise
  private pendingRequests: Map> = new Map();

  constructor(config: SdkConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.baseUrl = config.baseUrl || BASE_URL;
  }

  /**
   * 生成请求去重键
   */
  private getRequestKey(url: string, options: any): string {
    const bodyStr = options.body ? JSON.stringify(options.body) : '';
    return `${options.method || 'GET'}|${url}|${bodyStr}`;
  }

  /**
   * 发送请求（带去重）
   */
  private async request(path: string, options: any = {}): Promise<{ success: boolean; data?: T; error?: string; fromCache?: boolean }> {
    // 检查 path 是否已经是完整 URL
    let url: URL;
    if (path.startsWith('http://') || path.startsWith('https://')) {
      url = new URL(path);
    } else {
      const normalizedPath = path.startsWith('/') ? path : `/${path}`;
      const baseUrl = this.baseUrl.endsWith('/') ? this.baseUrl : `${this.baseUrl}/`;
      url = new URL(`${baseUrl}${normalizedPath}`);
    }

    if (this.config.apiKey) {
      url.searchParams.set('apiKey', this.config.apiKey);
      url.searchParams.set('appId', this.config.appId);
    }

    if (options.params) {
      Object.keys(options.params).forEach(key =>
        url.searchParams.append(key, String(options.params[key]))
      );
    }

    const urlStr = url.toString();
    const reqKey = this.getRequestKey(urlStr, options);

    // 请求去重：如果同一请求正在飞行中，直接复用其 Promise
    if (this.pendingRequests.has(reqKey)) {
      return this.pendingRequests.get(reqKey)!;
    }

    const isFormData = options.body instanceof FormData;

    const fetchOptions: RequestInit = {
      method: options.method || 'GET',
      headers: {
        'X-API-Key': this.config.apiKey,
        ...options.headers
      },
    };

    if (options.body) {
      if (isFormData) {
        if (fetchOptions.headers) {
          delete (fetchOptions.headers as any)['Content-Type'];
        }
        fetchOptions.body = options.body as FormData;
      } else {
        (fetchOptions.headers as any)['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
        fetchOptions.body = JSON.stringify(options.body);
      }
    }

    const controller = new AbortController();
    const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), this.config.timeout || 30000);
    fetchOptions.signal = controller.signal;

    const promise = (async () => {
      try {
        const response = await fetch(urlStr, fetchOptions);
        clearTimeout(timeoutId);

        const responseText = await response.text();
        let data: any;
        try {
          data = JSON.parse(responseText);
        } catch (e) {
          // 如果无法解析 JSON，且状态码是 200，说明可能返回了非 JSON 但成功的响应
          if (response.ok) {
            return { success: true, data: responseText as any };
          }
          throw new Error(`服务器返回了非 JSON 格式的内容: ${responseText.slice(0, 100)}...`);
        }

        if (!response.ok) {
          // 兼容不同的错误字段
          const errorMsg = data.message || data.error || data.msg || `HTTP ${response.status}`;
          throw new Error(errorMsg);
        }

        // 如果后端返回了标准的 { success: false, message: '...' } 格式，也抛出异常
        if (data && data.success === false) {
          throw new Error(data.message || data.error || data.msg || '操作失败');
        }

        // 自动缓存成功的数据
        if (options.cacheKey) {
          await storage.setItem(options.cacheKey, JSON.stringify(data));
        }

        // 自动解密敏感字段
        return { success: true, data: this.decryptData(data) };
      } catch (error: any) {
        // 尝试加载缓存
        if (options.cacheKey) {
          const cached = await storage.getItem(options.cacheKey);
          if (cached) {
            try {
              return { success: true, data: this.decryptData(JSON.parse(cached)), fromCache: true };
            } catch (e) {
              // ignore
            }
          }
        }
        return { success: false, error: error.message };
      } finally {
        // 请求完成后从去重池中移除
        this.pendingRequests.delete(reqKey);
      }
    })();

    this.pendingRequests.set(reqKey, promise);
    return promise;
  }

  /**
   * 递归解密对象中的敏感字段
   */
  private decryptData(data: any): any {
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') return data;

    if (Array.isArray(data)) {
      return data.map(item => this.decryptData(item));
    }

    const result = { ...data };
    Object.keys(result).forEach(key => {
      if (typeof result[key] === 'string') {
        result[key] = decryptStr(result[key]);
      } else if (typeof result[key] === 'object') {
        result[key] = this.decryptData(result[key]);
      }
    });
    return result;
  }

  /**
   * 获取App完整配置
   */
  async getConfig() {
    return this.request(`/config/${this.config.appId}`, { cacheKey: `config_${this.config.appId}` });
  }

  /**
   * 检查版本更新
   */
  async checkVersion(platform: string, currentVersion: string) {
    return this.request(`/version/${this.config.appId}`, { 
      params: { platform, version: currentVersion }
    });
  }

  /**
   * 验证API密钥有效性
   */
  async validateKey() {
    return this.request('/validate-key', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { appId: this.config.appId, apiKey: this.config.apiKey }
    });
  }

  /**
   * 获取功能开关
   */
  async getFeatureFlags() {
    return this.request(`/features/${this.config.appId}`, { cacheKey: `features_${this.config.appId}` });
  }

  /**
   * 获取存储配置 (CFR2等)
   */
  async getStorageConfig() {
    const res = await this.getConfig();
    if (res.success && res.data) {
      return {
        success: true,
        data: {
          cfr2: (res.data as any).cfr2,
          storage: (res.data as any).storage
        }
      };
    }
    return { success: false, error: res.error || '获取存储配置失败' };
  }

  async getMediaItems(params: any) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/list' : '/app-media/list';
    return this.request(endpoint, { params, cacheKey: `media_list_${JSON.stringify(params)}` });
  }

  async getMediaDetail(id: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-media/detail/${id}` : `/app-media/detail/${id}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { cacheKey: `media_detail_${id}` });
  }

  async deleteMedia(id: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-media/delete/${id}` : `/app-media/delete/${id}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { method: 'DELETE' });
  }

  async deleteAlbum(id: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-albums/delete/${id}` : `/app-albums/delete/${id}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { method: 'DELETE' });
  }

  async getRandomMedia(params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/random' : '/app-media/random';
    return this.request(endpoint, { params });
  }

  async getDailyGallery() {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/daily' : '/app-media/daily';
    return this.request(endpoint, { cacheKey: 'daily_gallery' });
  }

  async getWallpapers(params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/wallpapers' : '/app-media/wallpapers';
    return this.request(endpoint, { params });
  }

  /**
   * 搜索作品
   */
  async searchMedia(query: string, params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/search' : '/app-media/search';
    return this.request(endpoint, { 
      params: { ...params, q: query },
      cacheKey: `search_${query}_${JSON.stringify(params)}`
    });
  }

  /**
   * 获取热门搜索标签
   */
  async getTrendingTags() {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/trending-tags' : '/app-media/trending-tags';
    return this.request(endpoint, { cacheKey: 'trending_tags' });
  }

  async getPhotoAlbums(params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-albums/list' : '/app-albums/list';
    return this.request(endpoint, { params, cacheKey: `albums_list_${JSON.stringify(params)}` });
  }

  async getAlbumPhotos(albumId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-albums/photos/${albumId}` : `/app-albums/photos/${albumId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { cacheKey: `album_photos_${albumId}` });
  }

  async getCategories() {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-categories' : '/app-categories';
    return this.request(endpoint, { cacheKey: 'categories' });
  }

  /**
   * 获取所有标签
   */
  async getTags(params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-tags' : '/app-tags';
    return this.request(endpoint, { params, cacheKey: `tags_${JSON.stringify(params)}` });
  }

  async getCheckInStatus(userId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-user/checkin-status?userId=${userId}` : `/app-user/checkin-status?userId=${userId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint);
  }

  async performCheckIn(userId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-user/perform-checkin' : '/app-user/perform-checkin';
    return this.request(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { userId }
    });
  }

  async uploadFile(bucket: string, body: FormData): Promise<{ success: boolean; data?: any; error?: string }> {
    const { success, data: config } = await this.getStorageConfig();
    const storageConfig = success && config ? { ...(config as any).cfr2, ...(config as any).storage } : null;

    // 1. 尝试直接通过 Worker 上传 (性能最好)
    if (storageConfig && storageConfig.r2_mode === 'worker' && storageConfig.r2_worker_url) {
      try {
        const r2WorkerUrl = storageConfig.r2_worker_url.endsWith('/') ? storageConfig.r2_worker_url : `${storageConfig.r2_worker_url}/`;
        const response = await fetch(`${r2WorkerUrl}upload`, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: {
            'Authorization': storageConfig.r2_worker_token ? `Bearer ${storageConfig.r2_worker_token}` : '',
          },
          body: body
        });

        if (response.ok) {
          const res = await response.json();
          if (res.success) return { success: true, data: res as any };
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('Direct worker upload failed, falling back to gateway...', e);
      }
    }

    // 2. 备用方案：通过云函数网关上传
    const r2Endpoint = 'https://supabase.wo58.cn/functions/v1/app-storage';
    return this.request(r2Endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 
        'x-bucket-name': bucket,
        'x-api-key': this.config.apiKey
      },
      body: body
    });
  }

  async getComments(mediaId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-media/comments/${mediaId}` : `/app-media/comments/${mediaId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint);
  }

  async postComment(mediaId: string, userId: string, content: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/comments' : '/app-media/comments';
    return this.request(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { mediaId, userId, content }
    });
  }

  // User & Permission Modes
  async getUserProfile(userId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-user/profile?userId=${userId}` : `/app-user/profile?userId=${userId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { cacheKey: `user_profile_${userId}` });
  }

  async toggleFavorite(userId: string, mediaId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-user/toggle-favorite' : '/app-user/toggle-favorite';
    return this.request(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { userId, mediaId }
    });
  }

  async checkFavoriteStatus(userId: string, mediaId: string) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-user/favorite-status?userId=${userId}&mediaId=${mediaId}` : `/app-user/favorite-status?userId=${userId}&mediaId=${mediaId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint);
  }

  async getUserFavorites(userId: string, params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-user/favorites?userId=${userId}` : `/app-user/favorites?userId=${userId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { params });
  }

  async getUserMedia(userId: string, params: any = {}) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? `../../app-user/media?userId=${userId}` : `/app-user/media?userId=${userId}`;
    return this.request(endpoint, { params });
  }

  // Permission Mode
  async getPermissions(userId: string): Promise<{
    success: boolean;
    role?: string;
    group?: any;
    permissions?: string[];
    error?: string;
  }> {
    const res = await this.getUserProfile(userId);
    if (res.success && res.data) {
      const data = res.data as any;
      return {
        success: true,
        role: data.role,
        group: data.permission_groups,
        permissions: data.permission_groups?.permissions || []
      };
    }
    return { success: false, error: res.error || '获取权限失败' };
  }

  async checkPermission(userId: string, permission: string) {
    const res = await this.getPermissions(userId);
    if (res.success) {
      return res.permissions?.includes(permission) || res.role === 'admin';
    }
    return false;
  }

  // Upload Mode
  async uploadMedia(data: {
    userId: string;
    url: string;
    type?: string;
    title?: string;
    description?: string;
    categoryId?: string;
    tags?: string[];
    status?: string;
  }) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-media/upload' : '/app-media/upload';
    return this.request(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: data
    });
  }

  // Auth Mode
  async login(credentials: any): Promise<{ success: boolean; data?: any; error?: string }> {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-auth/login' : '/app-auth/login';
    const res = await this.request(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { ...credentials, action: 'login' }
    });
    
    // 兼容后端返回格式：{ success: true, data: { user, token } } 或直接是 { user, token }
    if (res.success && res.data) {
      const data = res.data as any;
      if (data.success === false) {
        return { success: false, error: data.message || data.error || '登录失败' };
      }
    }
    return res as any;
  }

  async register(userData: any) {
    const endpoint = this.baseUrl.includes('app-management') ? '../../app-auth/register' : '/app-auth/register';
    return this.request(endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { ...userData, action: 'register' }
    });
  }

  async signUp(body: any) {
    return this.register(body);
  }

  async signOut() {
    await storage.deleteItem('app_session');
    return { success: true };
  }

  async getSession() {
    const cached = await storage.getItem('app_session');
    return cached ? JSON.parse(cached) : null;
  }

  async saveSession(session: any) {
    await storage.setItem('app_session', JSON.stringify(session));
  }

  /**
   * 获取所有公开App列表
   */
  async getPublicApps() {
    return this.request('/all-apps');
  }

  /**
   * 导出APK打包配置
   */
  async exportBuildConfig() {
    return this.request(`/export-build-config/${this.config.appId}`);
  }
}

/**
 * 主题工具函数
 */
export function applyTheme(theme: Record, root?: any) {
  if (typeof document === 'undefined') return;
  const target = root || document.documentElement;
  Object.entries(theme).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    const cssVar = `--app-${kebabCase(key)}`;
    target.style.setProperty(cssVar, value);
  });
}

function kebabCase(str: string): string {
  return str.replace(/([A-Z])/g, '-$1').toLowerCase();
}

/**
 * 快捷初始化函数
 */
export async function initApp(config: SdkConfig) {
  const manager = new AppManager(config);

  // 1. 验证密钥
  const keyInfo = await manager.validateKey();
  if (!keyInfo.success || !(keyInfo.data as any)?.valid) {
    throw new Error(`API Key无效: ${keyInfo.error || (keyInfo.data as any)?.message}`);
  }

  // 2. 获取配置
  const configRes = await manager.getConfig();
  const configData = configRes.data as AppConfig;
  if (!configRes.success || !configRes.data) {
    throw new Error(`获取App配置失败: ${configRes.error}`);
  }

  // 3. 获取功能开关
  const featuresRes = await manager.getFeatureFlags();

  // 4. 应用主题
  if (configData.theme && typeof document !== 'undefined') {
    applyTheme(configData.theme);
  }

  return {
    success: true,
    manager,
    config: configData,
    features: (featuresRes.data || {}) as FeatureFlags,
    keyInfo: keyInfo.data,
  };
}

export const saveSDKConfig = async (config: SdkConfig) => {
  await secureStorage.setItem('sdk_app_id', config.appId);
  await secureStorage.setItem('sdk_api_key', config.apiKey);
  if (config.baseUrl) {
    await secureStorage.setItem('sdk_base_url', config.baseUrl);
  } else {
    await secureStorage.deleteItem('sdk_base_url');
  }
};

export const getSDKConfig = async (): Promise => {
  const appId = await secureStorage.getItem('sdk_app_id');
  const apiKey = await secureStorage.getItem('sdk_api_key');
  const baseUrl = await secureStorage.getItem('sdk_base_url');
  
  if (appId && apiKey) {
    return { 
      appId, 
      apiKey, 
      baseUrl: baseUrl || BASE_URL,
    };
  }
  return null;
};

export const clearSDKConfig = async () => {
  await secureStorage.deleteItem('sdk_app_id');
  await secureStorage.deleteItem('sdk_api_key');
  await secureStorage.deleteItem('sdk_base_url');
};

export function useAppConfig(sdkConfig: SdkConfig) {
  const [appConfig, setAppConfig] = useState(null);
  const [features, setFeatures] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const manager = new AppManager(sdkConfig);
      const configRes = await manager.getConfig();
      const featuresRes = await manager.getFeatureFlags();
      
      if (configRes.success && configRes.data) {
        setAppConfig(configRes.data as AppConfig);
      }
      if (featuresRes.success && featuresRes.data) {
        setFeatures(featuresRes.data as FeatureFlags);
      }
      
      if (!configRes.success) {
        setError(configRes.error || '获取配置失败');
      }
    } catch (e: any) {
      setError(e.message);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, [sdkConfig.appId, sdkConfig.apiKey]);

  useEffect(() => {
    refresh();
  }, [refresh]);

  return { appConfig, features, loading, error, refresh };
}内容完善相关云函数和页面数据， 
</action>

     9 function createResponse(data, status = 200) {
    10   return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {

    12     status,

    16 function getSupabaseClient() {
    17   const url = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') || '';
    18   const key = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') || '';
    19   return createClient(url, key);

    22 async function validateRequest(supabase, url, req) {
    23   const apiKey = url.searchParams.get('apiKey') || req.headers.get('x-api-key') || '';
    24   const appId = url.searchParams.get('appId') || '';

    35

    37   return { valid: true, keyData: data };

     8 
     9 function createResponse(data, status = 200) {
    10   return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
    11     headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    12     status,
    13   });
    14 }
    15 
    16 function getSupabaseClient() {
    17   const url = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') || '';
    18   const key = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') || '';
    19   return createClient(url, key);
    20 }
    21 
    22 async function validateRequest(supabase, url, req) {
    23   const apiKey = url.searchParams.get('apiKey') || req.headers.get('x-api-key') || '';
    24   const appId = url.searchParams.get('appId') || '';
    25 
    26   if (!apiKey || !appId) return { valid: false, message: 'Missing apiKey or appId' };
    27 
    28   const { data, error } = await supabase
    29     .from('app_api_keys')
    30     .select('id, permissions, expires_at')
    31     .eq('app_id', appId)
    32     .eq('api_key', apiKey)
    33     .eq('is_active', true)
    34     .maybeSingle();
    35 
    36   if (error || !data) return { valid: false, message: 'Invalid API Key' };
    37   return { valid: true, keyData: data };
    38 }
    39 
    40 Deno.serve(async (req) => {

 const apiKey = url.searchParams.get('apiKey') || req.headers.get('x-api-key') || '';\n  const appId = url.searchParams.get('appId') || '';\n\n  if (!apiKey || !appId) return { valid: false, message: 'Missing apiKey or appId' };\n\n  const { data, error } = await supabase\n    .from('app_api_keys')\n    .select('id, permissions, expires_at')\n    .eq('app_id', appId)\n    .eq('api_key', apiKey)\n    .eq('is_active', true)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (error || !data) return { valid: false, message: 'Invalid API Key' };\n  return { valid: true, keyData: data };\n}\n\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });\n\n  const url = new URL(req.url);\n  const supabase = getSupabaseClient();\n  const validation = await validateRequest(supabase, url, req);\n\n  if (!validation.valid) {\n    return createResponse({ success: false, message: validation.message }, 403);\n  }\n\n  const path = url.pathname;\n  // 🔥 关键修复：兼容 action 参数\n  const action = url.searchParams.get('action');\n\n  try {\n    // 🔥 修复：支持 ?action=list\n    if (path.endsWith('/app-media') && action === 'list' || path.endsWith('/list')) {\n      const page = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('page') || '0');\n      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '10');\n      const type = url.searchParams.get('type') || 'all';\n      const categoryId = url.searchParams.get('categoryId') || 'all';\n      const sortBy = url.searchParams.get('sortBy') || 'latest';\n      const tagIdsStr = url.searchParams.get('tagIds') || '';\n      const tagIds = tagIdsStr ? tagIdsStr.split(',') : null;\n      const userId = url.searchParams.get('userId') || null;\n\n      const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc('get_optimized_media_items_v3', {\n        p_user_id: userId,\n        p_type: type,\n        p_category_id: categoryId,\n        p_tag_ids: tagIds,\n        p_sort_by: sortBy,\n        p_limit: limit,\n        p_offset: page * limit\n      });\n\n      if (error) throw error;\n\n      const items = (data || []).map((item) => ({\n        ...item,\n        profiles: item.username ? { username: item.username, avatar_url: item.avatar_url } : null,\n      }));\n\n      const total = items.length > 0 ? Number((items[0]).total_count) : 0;\n\n      return createResponse({\n        success: true,\n        data: items,\n        total\n      });\n    }\n\n    if (path.endsWith('/random')) {\n      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '10');\n      const type = url.searchParams.get('type') || 'image';\n      \n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .select('*, profiles!user_id(username, avatar_url)')\n        .eq('status', 'approved')\n        .eq('is_hidden', false)\n        .eq('type', type)\n        .limit(limit)\n        .order('heat_score', { ascending: false });\n\n      const shuffled = (data || []).sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data: shuffled });\n    }\n\n    if (path.endsWith('/daily')) {\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .select('*, profiles!user_id(username, avatar_url)')\n        .eq('daily_gallery_status', 'published')\n        .order('daily_gallery_date', { ascending: false })\n        .limit(50);\n\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data: data || [] });\n    }\n\n    if (path.endsWith('/wallpapers')) {\n      const page = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('page') || '0');\n      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '20');\n      \n      const { data, error, count } = await supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .select('*, profiles!user_id(username, avatar_url)', { count: 'exact' })\n        .eq('status', 'approved')\n        .eq('type', 'image')\n        .eq('is_hidden', false)\n        .order('created_at', { ascending: false })\n        .range(page * limit, (page + 1) * limit - 1);\n\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data: data || [], total: count });\n    }\n\n    if (path.includes('/detail/')) {\n      const id = path.split('/').pop();\n      if (!id) return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Missing media id' }, 400);\n\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .select('*, profiles!user_id(username, avatar_url), media_tags(tags(name))')\n        .eq('id', id)\n        .maybeSingle();\n\n      if (!data) return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Media not found' }, 404);\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data });\n    }\n\n    // 删除媒体（软删除）\n    if (req.method === 'DELETE' && path.split('/').length > 2) {\n      const id = path.split('/').pop();\n      if (!id) return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Missing media id' }, 400);\n\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .update({ deleted_at: new Date().toISOString() })\n        .eq('id', id)\n        .select()\n        .single();\n\n      if (error) return createResponse({ success: false, message: error.message }, 500);\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data, message: '删除成功' });\n    }\n\n    // 搜索媒体\n    if (path.endsWith('/search')) {\n      const query = url.searchParams.get('q') || '';\n      const page = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('page') || '0');\n      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '20');\n      const type = url.searchParams.get('type') || 'all';\n\n      if (!query.trim()) {\n        return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Missing search query' }, 400);\n      }\n\n      let dbQuery = supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .select('*, profiles!user_id(username, avatar_url), media_tags(tags(name))', { count: 'exact' })\n        .is('deleted_at', null)\n        .or(`title.ilike.%${query}%,description.ilike.%${query}%`);\n\n      if (type !== 'all') dbQuery = dbQuery.eq('type', type);\n\n      const { data, error, count } = await dbQuery\n        .order('created_at', { ascending: false })\n        .range(page * limit, (page + 1) * limit - 1);\n\n      if (error) throw error;\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data: data || [], total: count || 0 });\n    }\n\n    // 热门搜索标签\n    if (path.endsWith('/trending-tags')) {\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('tags')\n        .select('id, name, color, description, media_count')\n        .order('media_count', { ascending: false })\n        .limit(30);\n\n      if (error) throw error;\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data: data || [] });\n    }\n\n    if (path.includes('/comments/')) {\n      const mediaId = path.split('/').pop();\n      if (!mediaId) return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Missing mediaId' }, 400);\n\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('comments')\n        .select('*, profiles!user_id(username, avatar_url)')\n        .eq('media_id', mediaId)\n        .order('created_at', { ascending: true });\n\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data: data || [] });\n    }\n\n    if (path.endsWith('/comments') && req.method === 'POST') {\n      const body = await req.json();\n      const { mediaId, userId, content } = body;\n      if (!mediaId || !userId || !content) return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Missing fields' }, 400);\n\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('comments')\n        .insert({ media_id: mediaId, user_id: userId, content })\n        .select()\n        .single();\n\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data });\n    }\n\n    if (path.endsWith('/upload') && req.method === 'POST') {\n      const body = await req.json();\n      const { userId, url: mediaUrl, type, title, description, categoryId, tags } = body;\n      \n      if (!userId || !mediaUrl) {\n        return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or url' }, 400);\n      }\n\n      const { data, error } = await supabase\n        .from('media_items')\n        .insert({\n          user_id: userId,\n          url: mediaUrl,\n          type: type || 'image',\n          title: title || '未命名作品',\n          description: description || '',\n          category_id: categoryId,\n          status: 'pending',\n          tags: tags || []\n        })\n        .select()\n        .single();\n\n      return createResponse({ success: true, data });\n    }\n\n    return createResponse({ success: false, message: 'Action not found' }, 404);\n  } catch (err) {\n    return createResponse({ success: false, message: err.message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n"}]}

     4 export interface UploadOptions {
     5   file: File;

     7   storageConfig?: any;

    10 export async function uploadToStorage(options: UploadOptions) {
    11   let { file, path, storageConfig } = options;
    12   
    13   // 核心修复：对上传路径进行脱敏处理，防止由于中文字符导致的 "InvalidKey" 错误（特别是在 Cloudflare R2/Worker 环境下）
    14   const sanitizePath = (p: string) => {
    15     return p.split('/').map(part => {
    16       // 仅保留基础字符，中文字符替换为下划线
    17       const sanitized = part.replace(/[^\w.-]/g, '_');
    18       // 如果经过过滤后变成空字符串（例如纯中文名），则使用时间戳兜底
    19       return sanitized || `file_${Date.now()}`;
    20     }).join('/');
    21   };
    22   
    23   path = sanitizePath(path);
    24   
    25   // 获取存储优先级和配置
    26   const storagePriority = storageConfig?.storage_priority || 'r2_first'; // r2_first | supabase_first
    27   const r2Mode = storageConfig?.r2_mode || 'direct'; // direct | worker
    28   const workerUrl = storageConfig?.r2_worker_url;
    29   const workerToken = storageConfig?.r2_worker_token;
    30   
    31   const tryWorkerUpload = async () => {
    32     if (!workerUrl) return null;
    33     try {
    34       const baseUrl = workerUrl.endsWith('/') ? workerUrl.slice(0, -1) : workerUrl;
    35       
    36       // 优先尝试 POST /upload（与 app-storage 标准接口一致）
    37       const postUrl = `${baseUrl}/upload`;
    38       const formData = new FormData();
    39       formData.append('file', file);
    40       formData.append('fileName', path);
    41       
    42       const postHeaders: Record<string, string> = {
    43         'Authorization': `Bearer ${workerToken}`,
    44       };
    45       if (storageConfig?.bucket_name) {
    46         postHeaders['x-bucket-name'] = storageConfig.bucket_name;
    47       }
    48       
    49       console.log('[Upload] 尝试 Worker POST /upload:', postUrl);
    50       let response = await fetch(postUrl, {
    51         method: 'POST',
    52         headers: postHeaders,
    53         body: formData
    54       });
    55       
    56       if (response.ok) {
    57         const data = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));
    58         if (data.success) {
    59           console.log('[Upload] Worker POST /upload 成功:', data.url || data.fakeUrl);
    60           return { success: true, url: data.url || data.fakeUrl };
    61         }
    62       }
    63       
    64       // POST /upload 失败，尝试旧版 PUT 直接上传（兼容旧 Worker）
    65       console.warn('[Upload] Worker POST /upload 失败，尝试 PUT 直接上传...');
    66       const putUrl = `${baseUrl}/${path}`;
    67       response = await fetch(putUrl, {
    68         method: 'PUT',
    69         headers: {
    70           'Authorization': `Bearer ${workerToken}`,
    71           'Content-Type': file.type
    72         },
    73         body: file
    74       });
    75       
    76       if (!response.ok) {
    77         const errorText = await response.text().catch(() => 'No error text');
    78         console.error(`[Upload] Worker PUT 返回错误: ${response.status}`, errorText);
    79         throw new Error(`Worker upload failed: ${response.status}`);
    80       }
    81       
    82       let finalUrl = '';
    83       if (storageConfig?.custom_domain) {
    84         const domain = storageConfig.custom_domain.endsWith('/') ? storageConfig.custom_domain : storageConfig.custom_domain + '/';
    85         finalUrl = domain + path;
    86       } else {
    87         finalUrl = putUrl;
    88       }
    89       
    90       return { success: true, url: finalUrl };
    91     } catch (e) {
    92       console.error('Worker upload error:', e);
    93       return null;
    94     }
    95   };
    96 
    97   const tryR2S3Direct = async () => {
    98     // 尝试调用统一的 app-storage 云函数
    99     try {
   100       const formData = new FormData();
   101       formData.append('file', file);
   102       formData.append('fileName', path);
   103       if (storageConfig?.bucket_name) {
   104         formData.append('bucket', storageConfig.bucket_name);
   105       }
   106       
   107       const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('app-storage', { 
   108         body: formData,
   109         headers: {
   110           'x-bucket-name': storageConfig?.bucket_name || ''
   111         }
   112       });
   113       
   114       if (error || !data?.success) {
   115         return null;
   116       }
   117       return data;
   118     } catch (e) {
   119       return null;
   120     }
   121   };
   122 
   123   const trySupabase = async () => {
   124     try {
   125       const { data, error } = await supabase.storage
   126         .from('media_content')
   127         .upload(path, file, {
   128           cacheControl: '3600',
   129           upsert: true
   130         });
   131       
   132       if (error) throw error;
   133       
   134       const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabase.storage
   135         .from('media_content')
   136         .getPublicUrl(path);
   137         
   138       return { success: true, url: publicUrl };
   139     } catch (e) {
   140       return null;
   141     }
   142   };
   143 
   144   // 执行策略
   145   console.log(`[Upload] 优先级: ${storagePriority}, 模式: ${r2Mode}, 文件: ${path}`);
   146   
   147   if (storagePriority === 'r2_first') {
   148     // 尝试 R2/Worker
   149     if (r2Mode === 'worker') {
   150       console.log('[Upload] 尝试 Worker 上传...');
   151       const res = await tryWorkerUpload();
   152       if (res) {
   153         console.log('[Upload] Worker 上传成功:', res.url);
   154         return res;
   155       }
   156       console.warn('[Upload] Worker 上传失败或未配置，正在回退到 Supabase...');
   157       toast.error('Worker 存储上传失败，将尝试回退到 Supabase');
   158     } else {
   159       console.log('[Upload] 尝试 R2/S3 直连上传...');
   160       const res = await tryR2S3Direct();
   161       if (res) {
   162         console.log('[Upload] R2/S3 直连上传成功:', res.url);
   163         return res;
   164       }
   165       console.warn('[Upload] R2/S3 直连上传失败或未配置，正在回退到 Supabase...');
   166       toast.error('R2 直连上传失败，将尝试回退到 Supabase');
   167     }
   168     // Fallback to Supabase
   169     const supabaseRes = await trySupabase();
   170     if (supabaseRes?.success) {
   171       console.log('[Upload] 回退到 Supabase 上传成功');
   172     }
   173     return supabaseRes;
   174   } else {
   175     // Supabase First
   176     console.log('[Upload] 优先尝试 Supabase 上传...');
   177     const res = await trySupabase();
   178     if (res) {
   179       console.log('[Upload] Supabase 上传成功:', res.url);
   180       return res;
   181     }
   182     // Fallback to R2
   183     console.warn('[Upload] Supabase 上传失败，尝试回退到 R2...');
   184     toast.error('Supabase 存储失败，正在尝试回退到云端存储');
   185     if (r2Mode === 'worker') {
   186       return await tryWorkerUpload() || { success: false, url: '' };
   187     } else {
   188       return await tryR2S3Direct() || { success: false, url: '' };
   189     }
   190   }
   191 }

     4 const corsHeaders = {

     6   'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type, x-bucket-name',
     7   'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, GET, OPTIONS, PUT, DELETE',

    10 // AWS Signature V4 签名工具类
    11 class AWS4Signer {
    12   static async hmacSha256(key: CryptoKey | Uint8Array, data: Uint8Array): Promise<Uint8Array> {
    13     let cryptoKey: CryptoKey;
    14     if (key instanceof Uint8Array) {
    15       cryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
    16         'raw', key, { name: 'HMAC', hash: 'SHA-256' }, false, ['sign']
    17       );
    18     } else {
    19       cryptoKey = key;
    20     }
    21     const signature = await crypto.subtle.sign('HMAC', cryptoKey, data);
    22     return new Uint8Array(signature);
    23   }
    24 
    25   static async sha256(data: Uint8Array): Promise<string> {
    26     const hash = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
    27     return Array.from(new Uint8Array(hash))
    28       .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
    29       .join('');
    30   }
    31 
    32   static async getSignatureKey(key: string, dateStamp: string, regionName: string, serviceName: string): Promise<Uint8Array> {
    33     const kDate = await this.hmacSha256(new TextEncoder().encode('AWS4' + key), new TextEncoder().encode(dateStamp));
    34     const kRegion = await this.hmacSha256(kDate, new TextEncoder().encode(regionName));
    35     const kService = await this.hmacSha256(kRegion, new TextEncoder().encode(serviceName));
    36     const kSigning = await this.hmacSha256(kService, new TextEncoder().encode('aws4_request'));
    37     return kSigning;
    38   }
    39 }
    40 
    41 async function validateRequest(supabase: any, url: URL, req: Request) {
    42   const authHeader = req.headers.get('authorization') || '';
    43   const apiKey = url.searchParams.get('apiKey') || req.headers.get('x-api-key') || '';
    44   const appId = url.searchParams.get('appId') || '';
    45 
    46   // 1. 优先尝试 Supabase Auth 验证（内部调用，来自 supabase.functions.invoke）
    47   if (authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ') && !apiKey) {
    48     try {
    49       const token = authHeader.replace('Bearer ', '');
    50       const { data: { user }, error } = await supabase.auth.getUser(token);
    51       if (user && !error) {
    52         // 验证用户是否为管理员
    53         const { data: profile } = await supabase
    54           .from('profiles')
    55           .select('role')
    56           .eq('id', user.id)
    57           .maybeSingle();
    58         if (profile?.role === 'admin') {
    59           return { valid: true, keyData: { permissions: ['admin'], user_id: user.id } };
    60         }
    61       }
    62     } catch (e) {
    63       console.log('[AppStorage] Auth validation error:', e);
    64     }
    65   }
    66 
    67   // 2. API Key 验证（外部应用调用）
    68   if (!apiKey || !appId) return { valid: false, message: 'Missing apiKey or appId' };
    69 
    70   const { data, error } = await supabase
    71     .from('app_api_keys')
    72     .select('id, permissions, expires_at')
    73     .eq('app_id', appId)
    74     .eq('api_key', apiKey)
    75     .eq('is_active', true)
    76     .maybeSingle();
    77 
    78   if (error || !data) return { valid: false, message: 'Invalid API Key' };
    79   if (data.expires_at && new Date(data.expires_at).getTime() < Date.now()) {
    80     return { valid: false, message: 'API Key expired' };
    81   }
    82 
    83   return { valid: true, keyData: data };
    84 }
    85 
    86 serve(async (req: Request) => {
    87   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    88     return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders })
    89   }
    90 
    91   const url = new URL(req.url);
    92   try {
    93     const supabaseUrl = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!;
    94     const supabaseServiceKey = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!;
    95     const supabaseClient = createClient(supabaseUrl, supabaseServiceKey);
    96 
    97     const validation = await validateRequest(supabaseClient, url, req);
    98     if (!validation.valid) {
    99       return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, message: validation.message }), { status: 403, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   100     }
   101 
   102     // 1. 获取存储配置
   103     const { data: config } = await supabaseClient
   104       .from('storage_configs')
   105       .select('*')
   106       .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
   107       .limit(1)
   108       .maybeSingle();
   109 
   110     if (!config) {
   111       throw new Error('未发现存储配置');
   112     }
   113 
   114     // 2. 解析请求
   115     const formData = await req.formData();
   116     const file = formData.get('file') as File;
   117     const fileName = formData.get('fileName') as string;
   118     const headerBucket = req.headers.get('x-bucket-name');
   119     const formBucket = formData.get('bucket') as string;
   120     const targetBucket = headerBucket || formBucket || config.bucket_name || 'media_content';
   121 
   122     if (!file || !fileName) {
   123       throw new Error('缺少文件或文件名');
   124     }
   125 
   126     const fileBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
   127     const fileBytes = new Uint8Array(fileBuffer);
   128     const contentType = file.type || 'application/octet-stream';
   129 
   130     // 3. 按照优先级尝试存储方式
   131     // 优先级 1: S3 直连配置
   132     const hasS3Config = config.endpoint && config.key_id && config.secret_key && config.bucket_name;
   133     if (hasS3Config) {
   134       console.log('[AppStorage] Using S3 Direct mode');
   135       try {
   136         const { endpoint, key_id, secret_key, custom_domain } = config;
   137         const endpointUrl = new URL(endpoint);
   138         const host = endpointUrl.hostname;
   139         const region = 'auto';
   140         const service = 's3';
   141         const amzDate = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:-]|\.\d{3}/g, '');
   142         const dateStamp = amzDate.slice(0, 8);
   143         
   144         const canonicalUri = `/${targetBucket}/${fileName}`;
   145         const encodedUri = canonicalUri.split('/').map(s => encodeURIComponent(s)).join('/');
   146         const payloadHash = await AWS4Signer.sha256(fileBytes);
   147         const canonicalHeaders = `cache-control:public, max-age=86400\ncontent-type:${contentType}\nhost:${host}\nx-amz-content-sha256:${payloadHash}\nx-amz-date:${amzDate}\n`;
   148         const signedHeaders = 'cache-control;content-type;host;x-amz-content-sha256;x-amz-date';
   149         const canonicalRequest = ['PUT', encodedUri, '', canonicalHeaders, signedHeaders, payloadHash].join('\n');
   150         const credentialScope = `${dateStamp}/${region}/${service}/aws4_request`;
   151         const stringToSign = ['AWS4-HMAC-SHA256', amzDate, credentialScope, await AWS4Signer.sha256(new TextEncoder().encode(canonicalRequest))].join('\n');
   152         const signingKey = await AWS4Signer.getSignatureKey(secret_key, dateStamp, region, service);
   153         const signatureArr = await AWS4Signer.hmacSha256(signingKey, new TextEncoder().encode(stringToSign));
   154         const signature = Array.from(signatureArr).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
   155         
   156         const uploadUrl = `${endpoint.replace(/\/+$/, '')}${encodedUri}`;
   157         const uploadRes = await fetch(uploadUrl, {
   158           method: 'PUT',
   159           headers: {
   160             'Host': host,
   161             'x-amz-date': amzDate,
   162             'x-amz-content-sha256': payloadHash,
   163             'Authorization': `AWS4-HMAC-SHA256 Credential=${key_id}/${credentialScope}, SignedHeaders=${signedHeaders}, Signature=${signature}`,
   164             'Content-Type': contentType,
   165             'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=86400',
   166           },
   167           body: fileBytes
   168         });
   169 
   170         if (uploadRes.ok) {
   171           const publicUrl = custom_domain ? `${custom_domain.replace(/\/+$/, '')}/${fileName}` : `${endpoint.replace(/\/+$/, '')}/${targetBucket}/${fileName}`;
   172           return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, url: publicUrl, mode: 's3' }), { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   173         }
   174         console.warn('[AppStorage] S3 upload failed, trying next method...');
   175       } catch (e) {
   176         console.error('[AppStorage] S3 error:', e);
   177       }
   178     }
   179 
   180     // 优先级 2: Worker 模式
   181     const hasWorkerConfig = config.r2_worker_url && config.r2_worker_token;
   182     if (hasWorkerConfig) {
   183       console.log('[AppStorage] Using Worker mode');
   184       try {
   185         const workerFormData = new FormData();
   186         workerFormData.append('file', file);
   187         workerFormData.append('fileName', fileName);
   188         
   189         const uploadRes = await fetch(`${config.r2_worker_url.replace(/\/$/, '')}/upload`, {
   190           method: 'POST',
   191           headers: {
   192             'Authorization': `Bearer ${config.r2_worker_token}`,
   193             'x-bucket-name': targetBucket
   194           },
   195           body: workerFormData
   196         });
   197 
   198         if (uploadRes.ok) {
   199           const data = await uploadRes.json();
   200           if (data.success) {
   201             return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, url: data.url || data.fakeUrl, mode: 'worker' }), { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   202           }
   203         }
   204         console.warn('[AppStorage] Worker upload failed, trying next method...');
   205       } catch (e) {
   206         console.error('[AppStorage] Worker error:', e);
   207       }
   208     }
   209 
   210     // 优先级 3: Supabase 兜底
   211     console.log('[AppStorage] Falling back to Supabase Storage');
   212     const { data: uploadData, error: upError } = await supabaseClient.storage
   213       .from('media_content')
   214       .upload(fileName, fileBytes, { contentType, upsert: true });
   215 
   216     if (upError) throw upError;
   217 
   218     const { data: { publicUrl } } = supabaseClient.storage.from('media_content').getPublicUrl(fileName);
   219     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: true, url: publicUrl, mode: 'supabase' }), { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   220 
   221   } catch (error: any) {
   222     return new Response(JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: error.message }), { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } });
   223   }
   224 })

New String: ```
export interface UploadOptions {
  file: File;
  path: string;
  storageConfig?: any;
}

/**
 * 验证 URL 是否真实可访问（主要用于图片）
 * 使用 Image 对象验证图片，非图片使用 fetch HEAD
 */
function verifyUrl(url: string, timeout = 2000): Promise<boolean> {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => resolve(false), timeout);
    // 图片 URL：使用 Image 对象验证（能准确检测 404）
    if (/\.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|webp|svg|bmp|ico)(\?.*)?$/i.test(url)) {
      const img = new Image();
      img.onload = () => { clearTimeout(timer); resolve(true); };
      img.onerror = () => { clearTimeout(timer); resolve(false); };
      img.src = url;
    } else {
      // 非图片：使用 fetch HEAD（no-cors 模式，至少验证域名可达）
      fetch(url, { method: 'HEAD', mode: 'no-cors' })
        .then(() => { clearTimeout(timer); resolve(true); })
        .catch(() => { clearTimeout(timer); resolve(false); });
    }
  });
}

export async function uploadToStorage(options: UploadOptions) {

        return null;
      }
      // 云函数返回成功时，额外验证 URL 是否真实可访问（防御 Worker 返回假成功）
      if (data.url) {
        const isValid = await verifyUrl(data.url);
        if (!isValid) {
          console.warn('[Upload] app-storage 返回的 URL 验证失败:', data.url);
          return null;
        }
      }
      return data;
    } catch (e) {
      return null;
    }
  };
```

</action>

   544     if (verifyingRef.current) return;
   545     
   546     // 防止过于频繁的并发请求

   548       console.log('[DailyGallery] Verifying too frequent, ignoring...');
   549       return;
   550     }
   551

   559     }

   563
